      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Belarus_at_the_Olympics" title="Belarus at the Olympics">Belarus at the Olympics</a>
      </div> 
      <p>Belarus has competed in the Olympic Games since the <a href="/wiki/1994_Winter_Olympics" title="1994 Winter Olympics">1994 Winter Olympics</a> as an independent nation. Receiving heavy sponsorship from the government, <a href="/wiki/Ice_hockey" title="Ice hockey">ice hockey</a> is the nation's second most popular sport after <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Belarus_national_football_team" title="Belarus national football team">national football team</a> has never qualified for a major tournament; however, <a href="/wiki/FC_BATE_Borisov" title="FC BATE Borisov">BATE Borisov</a> has played in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Belarus_national_men%27s_ice_hockey_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Belarus national men's ice hockey team">national hockey team</a> finished fourth at the <a href="/wiki/Ice_hockey_at_the_2002_Winter_Olympics" title="Ice hockey at the 2002 Winter Olympics">2002 Salt Lake City Olympics</a> following a memorable upset win over Sweden in the quarterfinals, and regularly competes in the <a href="/wiki/Ice_Hockey_World_Championships" title="Ice Hockey World Championships">World Championships</a>, often making the quarterfinals. Numerous Belarusian players are present in the <a href="/wiki/Kontinental_Hockey_League" title="Kontinental Hockey League">Kontinental Hockey League</a> in Eurasia, particularly for Belarusian club <a href="/wiki/HC_Dinamo_Minsk" title="HC Dinamo Minsk">HC Dinamo Minsk</a>, and several have also played in the <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">National Hockey League</a> in North America. <a href="/wiki/Darya_Domracheva" title="Darya Domracheva">Darya Domracheva</a> is a leading <a href="/wiki/Biathlon" title="Biathlon">biathlete</a> whose honours include three gold medals at the <a href="/wiki/2014_Winter_Olympics" title="2014 Winter Olympics">2014 Winter Olympics</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">[232]</a></sup> </p> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Victoria_Azarenka_(18567208246).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Victoria_Azarenka_%2818567208246%29.jpg/220px-Victoria_Azarenka_%2818567208246%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="193" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Victoria_Azarenka_%2818567208246%29.jpg/330px-Victoria_Azarenka_%2818567208246%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Victoria_Azarenka_%2818567208246%29.jpg/440px-Victoria_Azarenka_%2818567208246%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4042" data-file-height="3541"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Victoria_Azarenka_(18567208246).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><a href="/wiki/Victoria_Azarenka" title="Victoria Azarenka">Victoria Azarenka</a>, professional <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a> player and a former <a href="/wiki/List_of_WTA_number_1_ranked_players" class="mw-redirect" title="List of WTA number 1 ranked players">world No. 1</a> in singles
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p><a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">Tennis</a> player <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Azarenka" title="Victoria Azarenka">Victoria Azarenka</a> became the first Belarusian to win a <a href="/wiki/Grand_Slam_(tennis)" title="Grand Slam (tennis)">Grand Slam</a> singles title at the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Open" title="Australian Open">Australian Open</a> in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">[233]</a></sup> She also won the gold medal in mixed doubles at the <a href="/wiki/Tennis_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Tennis at the 2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a> with <a href="/wiki/Max_Mirnyi" title="Max Mirnyi">Max Mirnyi</a>, who holds ten Grand Slam titles in <a href="/wiki/Singles_tennis" class="mw-redirect" title="Singles tennis">doubles</a>. </p>
      <p>Other notable Belarusian sportspeople include cyclist <a href="/wiki/Vasil_Kiryienka" title="Vasil Kiryienka">Vasil Kiryienka</a>, who won the <a href="/wiki/2015_UCI_Road_World_Championships_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_time_trial" title="2015 UCI Road World Championships – Men's time trial">2015 Road World Time Trial Championship</a>, and middle-distance runner <a href="/wiki/Maryna_Arzamasava" class="mw-redirect" title="Maryna Arzamasava">Maryna Arzamasava</a>, who won the gold medal in the <a href="/wiki/2015_World_Championships_in_Athletics_%E2%80%93_Women%27s_800_metres" title="2015 World Championships in Athletics – Women's 800 metres">800m at the 2015 World Championships in Athletics</a>. <a href="/wiki/Andrei_Arlovski" title="Andrei Arlovski">Andrei Arlovski</a>, who was born in <a href="/wiki/Babruysk" title="Babruysk">Babruysk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Byelorussian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Byelorussian Soviet Socialist Republic">Byelorussian SSR</a>, is a current <a href="/wiki/Ultimate_Fighting_Championship" title="Ultimate Fighting Championship">UFC</a> fighter and the former <a href="/wiki/List_of_UFC_champions" title="List of UFC champions">UFC heavyweight champion of the world</a>. </p>
      <p>Belarus is also known for its strong rhythmic gymnasts. Noticeable gymnasts include <a href="/wiki/Inna_Zhukova" title="Inna Zhukova">Inna Zhukova</a>, who earned silver at the <a href="/wiki/2008_Beijing_Olympics" class="mw-redirect" title="2008 Beijing Olympics">2008 Beijing Olympics</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liubov_Charkashyna" title="Liubov Charkashyna">Liubov Charkashyna</a>, who earned bronze at the 2012 London Olympics and <a href="/wiki/Melitina_Staniouta" title="Melitina Staniouta">Melitina Staniouta</a>, Bronze All-Around Medalist of the 2015 World Championships. The Belorussian senior group earned bronze at the <a href="/wiki/2012_London_Olympics" class="mw-redirect" title="2012 London Olympics">2012 London Olympics</a>. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Telecommunications">Telecommunications</span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Telecommunications_in_Belarus" title="Telecommunications in Belarus">Telecommunications in Belarus</a>
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Censorship_in_Belarus" title="Censorship in Belarus">Censorship in Belarus</a>
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>Country code: <a href="/wiki/.by" title=".by">.by</a></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>The state telecom monopoly, Beltelecom, holds the exclusive interconnection with Internet providers outside of Belarus. Beltelecom owns all the backbone channels that linked to the Lattelecom, TEO LT, <a href="/wiki/Tata_Communications" title="Tata Communications">Tata Communications</a> (former <a href="/wiki/Teleglobe" class="mw-redirect" title="Teleglobe">Teleglobe</a>), Synterra, <a href="/wiki/Rostelecom" title="Rostelecom">Rostelecom</a>, Transtelekom and MTS ISPs. Beltelecom is the only operator licensed to provide commercial VoIP services in Belarus.<sup id="cite_ref-ONI-Belarus-Nov2010_236-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ONI-Belarus-Nov2010-236">[234]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Heritage_Sites">World Heritage Sites</span></h3> 
      <p>Belarus has four <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a>-designated <a href="/wiki/World_Heritage_Site" title="World Heritage Site">World Heritage Sites</a>: the <a href="/wiki/Mir_Castle_Complex" title="Mir Castle Complex">Mir Castle Complex</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Nesvizh_Castle" title="Nesvizh Castle">Nesvizh Castle</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Bia%C5%82owie%C5%BCa_Forest" title="Białowieża Forest">Belovezhskaya Pushcha</a> (shared with <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>), and the <a href="/wiki/Struve_Geodetic_Arc" title="Struve Geodetic Arc">Struve Geodetic Arc</a> (shared with nine other countries).<sup id="cite_ref-UNSECO_237-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNSECO-237">[235]</a></sup> </p>

                 <div>
                  <div class="plainlist">
                   <ul>
                    <li><sup>1</sup> <a href="/wiki/Island#Oceanic_islands" title="Island">Oceanic islands</a> within the vicinity of Europe are usually grouped with the continent even though they are not situated on its continental shelf.</li>
                    <li><sup>2</sup> Some countries completely outside the conventional geographical boundaries of Europe are commonly associated with the continent due to ethnological links.</li>
                   </ul>
